< text>
Our old water heater was leaking and caused a bit of water damage in our garage. Joe was able to come and see what was going on and referred us to get the damage fixed and install the water heater.

Fast forward a couple weeks, where the construction company was fixing the dry wall and took it upon themselves to place the water heater. They ended up doing it wrong and we have no hot water for THREE days.

Joe stopped by to pick up the old water heater and looked at the job they did and was concerned because it was wrong (Joe was suppose to install it but the construction company for some reason did it). He took it upon himself to make sure that he fixed this ASAP. He made calls got us a completely new water heater and installed it himself in LESS than 20 hours. He was determined about getting this fixed for us because he know we had no hot water.

Joe and his team came in, did their magic and I went to wash dishes and burned my hand with hot water. I have never been so happy!

It was so nice to know he really cared, wanted to fix the situation and followed through with everything he said. If I have any future plumbing issues I am 100% going to call them. I could not be more happy with their promptness, professionalism, and knowledge.</text>

<userid>100664983864819439685</userid><Name>Piper Belmonte</Name><Time>1561410664302<//Time><rate>4< /rate>< text>
After getting quotes from 3 various other firms for a tankless warm water heating unit, I so desired to offer these folks 5 star. Their team as well as quote were educated and also very competitive. Their installment job was additionally exceptional. In spite of ensuring me that they would certainly draw the permit for the job (as well as that they 'd done so prior to) and take treatment of the succeeding city evaluation, they backed out after the contract was signed. According to them, the needs for my neighborhood consisted of an entire site strategy for the complicated rather than my just my townhouse - making it cost-prohibitive. They refunded the permit cost, but not the examination visit fee even with numerous call. They did make a follow-up visit to confirm the performance of my unit and their prices consisted of a two-year labor guarantee and a flush of the unit after the initial year. PERK SUGGESTIONS: 1) Tankless water heaters warmth water instantaneously, however do NOT provide instantaneous warm water (pipeline size in between heater and also faucet is still the exact same). 2) They are very gas efficient, but not cheaper to operate provided their 2-3x installation cost and also anticipated useful life. 3) They are a lot more conscious hard water than storage water heaters. If you do not install an inline filter\/softener (at more cost), they will die early and also cost you much more than regular water heater. 4) You TIN retrofit a Noritz EZ design tankless right into an older condo\/home that has a 3-4\" exhaust and a 3\/4\" gas line. 5) These are offered as packages by Residence Depot, Lowes, and so on so make your installer price match considering that they mark that number up by 20%.</text>

<Text>I'm a regular at this place. Gym has some positives but also negatives. Big place, tons of equipment. As big as it is, they manage to not have enough mat space during busy times. They take months to fix/maintain partially working equipment.

Phone reception here is really bad because there are high voltage transmission lines right outside - so that's not changing anytime soon, the gym should offer free wifi to make up for that. During busy hours you might have to park pretty far away, but usually there are still spots.

They have a great selection of free weights, unfortunately that is also what causes this gym to be drowning in bros, from the Santa Clarita hardbois to the San Fernando cholobros, bad tattoos for everyone. So if you want to use the weights you'll need to navigate bro culture, communicating with primate-like grunts and nods. They won't be racked or organized unless employees have time to do it, seems like once a day. And you won't be surprised to find equipment regularly damaged because someone used it incorrectly.

The bros also try their best to make the locker rooms and showers disgusting, while the staff occasionally cleans up after them. Grossest part is the smell in the bathrooms, my guess is that's related to the roiders (handicap stall seems to be a favorite place to shoot those btw).

Overall this gym appears to offer a lot due to the size, but in use it's like any normal size gym. For me there's more downsides than up, but it's close and gets the job done.<//Text>< Pictures>
